-   [<span data-ttu-id="1a238-930">Атрибуты</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1a238-930">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2003-r2-attributes)

## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="1a238-1611">Атрибуты Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1a238-1611">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1a238-1612">Этот класс содержит следующие атрибуты для Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1a238-1612">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
